if (is_file('includes/limits.inc.php') && (sha1_file('includes/limits.inc.php') != 'dc6c7c4cf35733fb9ecdfbe23906a93b528f5c7a')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/limits.inc.php');
	$tmp = pathinfo('includes/limits.inc.php');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/limits.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('includes/limits.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('includes/limits.inc.php')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/limits.inc.php');
} else if (sha1_file('includes/limits.inc.php') != 'dc6c7c4cf35733fb9ecdfbe23906a93b528f5c7a') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/limits.inc.php');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/limits.inc.php', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/limits.inc.php');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'db211b5d7b573c4a7cf4658f7e5ea7df30a058d1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'db211b5d7b573c4a7cf4658f7e5ea7df30a058d1') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '8feffe62e03631aa450786c4474375b21ab26d0f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'db211b5d7b573c4a7cf4658f7e5ea7df30a058d1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != '7932dedd7db741694b0480c834275f7ce7e19173') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '7932dedd7db741694b0480c834275f7ce7e19173') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '5ec5d86bd222c7bc672b2e6107d4aabed671d798') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '7932dedd7db741694b0480c834275f7ce7e19173') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');

			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '45fd2e34938c3af4f9ab80ba1a763df793aadbad') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') != '63e5f8add607e8c0d299b2632ff25f8156ed24ba') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') !== '63e5f8add607e8c0d299b2632ff25f8156ed24ba') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') !== 'e8a1149a7f26117e0b69832d6de869f45dd37fe1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') !== '63e5f8add607e8c0d299b2632ff25f8156ed24ba') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_15();
	if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php') != '55146017584d636edbf2a2be8e1f51072c510b64') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php') !== '55146017584d636edbf2a2be8e1f51072c510b64') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php') !== 'dc145c356f687ffeeaeea3cdec913e21d8d991eb') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php') !== '55146017584d636edbf2a2be8e1f51072c510b64') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
